  var options = {
    valueNames: [ 'title', 'url', 'location', 'department' ],
    item: '<li class="posting"><div class="title"></div><span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;</span><div class="location"></div><a class="url d-none job-post-url"></a></li>',
    page: 500
  };
  
  var jobsList = new List('jobs', options, values);
  
  console.log(jobsList)
  
  var selectedLocation   = 'All';
  var selectedDepartment = 'All';
  
  $(function(){
    filterJobs();
  });
  
  function filterJobs() {
    jobsList.filter(function(item) {
      if (
        (item.values().department == selectedDepartment && item.values().location.includes(selectedLocation))
        || (selectedDepartment == 'All' && selectedLocation == 'All')
        || (selectedLocation   == 'All' && item.values().department == selectedDepartment)
        || (selectedDepartment == 'All' && item.values().location.includes(selectedLocation))
        ) 
      {
        return true;
      } else {
        return false;
      }
    });
  
    if (jobsList.matchingItems.length == 0) {
      $(".job-listing .section-title").html("Sorry, all our flights are full for this search.");
    } else {
      $(".job-listing .section-title").html("Role:");
    }
  
    // update department counts
    $('ul.departments li, select.departments option').each(function() {
      dep = $( this ).data('depo');
      count = 0
      if (counts[selectedLocation][dep] != undefined) {
        count = counts[selectedLocation][dep];
      }
  
      $("ul.departments li[data-depo*='" + dep + "']").text(dep + ' (' + count + ')');
      $("select.departments option[data-depo*='" + dep + "']").text(dep + ' (' + count + ')');
    });
  
    // update location counts
    $('select.locations option').each(function() {
      loc = $(this).data('loc');
      count = 0
      if (counts[loc][selectedDepartment] != undefined) {
        count = counts[loc][selectedDepartment]
      }
      $("select.locations option[data-loc*='" + loc + "']").text(loc + ' (' + count + ')');
    });
  }
  
  $('.departments li').click(function() {
    $('.departments li').removeClass('active');
    $(this).addClass('active');
    selectedDepartment = $(this).data('depo');
    filterJobs();
  });
  
  $('select.departments').change(function() {
    selectedDepartment = $(this).children('option:selected').data('depo');
    filterJobs();
  });
  
  $('select.locations').change(function() {
    selectedLocation = $(this).children('option:selected').data('loc');
    filterJobs();
  });
  
  $(".posting").click(function() {
    trackEvent('careers','opening','click');
    console.log($(this).find('a').text());
    window.location = $(this).find('a').text();
  });
  
  loc = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('loc');
  if (loc) {
    selectedLocation = loc;
    $(".locations [data-loc*='" + loc + "']").attr('selected', 'selected');
    filterJobs();
  }
  
  dep = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('dep');
  if (dep) {
    selectedDepartment = dep;
    $('.departments li').removeClass('active');
    $(".departments [data-depo*='" + dep + "']").addClass('active');
    $("select.departments option[data-depo*='" + dep + "']").attr('selected', 'selected');
    filterJobs();
  }
</script>

  const demoButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.homepage-demo__modal')
  const body = document.body;
  
  for (const demoButton of demoButtons) {
    demoButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      body.classList.add('ta-modal-open');
    })
  }
  
  document.getElementById('closeForm').addEventListener('click', () => {
    body.classList.remove('ta-modal-open');
  })
  document.getElementById('modalPageMask').addEventListener('click', () => {
    body.classList.remove('ta-modal-open');
